====================================================================================================
NASIS Pedon Report for: area ---- Area

ACCEPT pedonid_list.
EXEC SQL SELECT

area.areatypeiidref/1 AS areatypeiidref,
area.seqnum AS seqnum,
area.areasymbol AS areasymbol,
area.areaname AS areaname,
area.areaacres AS areaacres,
area.obterm AS obterm,
area.recwlupdated AS recwlupdated,
area.recuseriidref/1 AS recuseriidref,
area.areaiid/1 AS areaiid

FROM pedon
RELATIONSHIP TO PEDON TABLE COULD NOT BE ESTABLISHED
INNER JOIN nasisgroup ON nasisgroup.nasissiteiidref=nasissite.nasissiteiid
INNER JOIN areatype ON areatype.grpiidref,atdbiidref=nasisgroup.grpiid,nasissiteiidref
INNER JOIN area ON area.areatypeiidref=areatype.areatypeiid;.

TEMPLATE area WIDTH UNLIMITED SEPARATOR"|"
AT LEFT FIELD SEPARATOR  "",
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD.

SECTION WHEN AT START
HEADING
AT LEFT "@begin area".
END SECTION.

SECTION HEADING
USING area
'areatypeiidref',
'seqnum',
'areasymbol',
'areaname',
'areaacres',
'obterm',
'recwlupdated',
'recuseriidref',
'areaiid'.

DATA
USING area
areatypeiidref,
seqnum,
areasymbol,
areaname,
areaacres,
obterm,
recwlupdated,
recuseriidref,
areaiid.
END SECTION.

SECTION WHEN NO DATA
DATA
AT LEFT "@begin area".
USING area
'areatypeiidref',
'seqnum',
'areasymbol',
'areaname',
'areaacres',
'obterm',
'recwlupdated',
'recuseriidref',
'areaiid'.
AT LEFT "@end".
END SECTION.

SECTION WHEN AT END DATA
AT LEFT "@end".
END SECTION.

INNER JOIN area ON area.areatypeiidref=areatype.areatypeiid
INNER JOIN areatext ON areatext.areaiidref=area.areaiid;.

NASIS Pedon Report for: basalareatreescounted ---- Basal Area Trees Counted

ACCEPT pedonid_list.
EXEC SQL SELECT

basalareatreescounted.plotspeciebasalareaiidref/1 AS plotspeciebasalareaiidref,
basalareatreescounted.seqnum AS seqnum,
basalareatreescounted.treenumber AS treenumber,
basalareatreescounted.treeheight AS treeheight,
basalareatreescounted.treediameterbreastheight AS treediameterbreastheight,
basalareatreescounted.recwlupdated AS recwlupdated,
basalareatreescounted.recuseriidref/1 AS recuseriidref,
basalareatreescounted.basalareatreescountediid/1 AS basalareatreescountediid

FROM pedon
RELATIONSHIP TO PEDON TABLE COULD NOT BE ESTABLISHED
INNER JOIN nasisgroup ON nasisgroup.nasissiteiidref=nasissite.nasissiteiid
INNER JOIN plant ON plant.grpiidref,plantdbiidref=nasisgroup.grpiid,nasissiteiidref
INNER JOIN plotspeciesbasalarea ON plotspeciesbasalarea.plantiidref=plant.plantiid
INNER JOIN basalareatreescounted ON basalareatreescounted.plotspeciebasalareaiidref=plotspeciesbasalarea.plotspeciebasalareaiid;.

TEMPLATE basalareatreescounted WIDTH UNLIMITED SEPARATOR"|"
AT LEFT FIELD SEPARATOR  "",
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD.

SECTION WHEN AT START
HEADING
AT LEFT "@begin basalareatreescounted".
END SECTION.

SECTION HEADING
USING basalareatreescounted
'plotspeciebasalareaiidref',
'seqnum',
'treenumber',
'treeheight',
'treediameterbreastheight',
'recwlupdated',
'recuseriidref',
'basalareatreescountediid'.

DATA
USING basalareatreescounted
plotspeciebasalareaiidref,
seqnum,
treenumber,

treediameterbreastheight,
recwlupdated,
recuseriidref,

END SECTION.

'treediameterbreastheight',

NASIS Pedon Report for: belttransectsummary ---- Belt Transect Summary

belttransectsummary.belttranssummiid/1 AS belttranssummiid

FROM pedon
INNER JOIN siteobs ON siteobs.siteiidref=site.siteiid
INNER JOIN pedon ON pedon.siteobsiidref=siteobs.siteobsiid AND peiid IN ($pedonid_list)
INNER JOIN vegtransect ON vegtransect.vegplotiidref=vegplot.vegplotiid
INNER JOIN belttransectsummary ON belttransectsummary.vegtransectiidref=vegtransect.vegtransectiid;.

'belttranssummiid'.

FROM pedon
RELATIONSHIP TO PEDON TABLE COULD NOT BE ESTABLISHED

INNER JOIN plant ON plant.grpiidref,plantdbiidref=nasisgroup.grpiid,nasissiteiidref
INNER JOIN vegtransectplantsummary ON vegtransectplantsummary.plantiidref=plant.plantiid
INNER JOIN nestedfreqquadratdetails ON nestedfreqquadratdetails.vegtransplantsummiidref=vegtransectplantsummary.vegtransplantsummiid;.

AT LEFT FIELD SEPARATOR  "",

'recwlupdated',
'recuseriidref',
'nestedfreqquaddetailsiid'.

====================================================================================================
NASIS Pedon Report for: vegplotrefecmdoc ---- Veg Plot Reference ECM Documents

ACCEPT pedonid_list.
EXEC SQL SELECT

vegplotrefecmdoc.vegplotiidref/1 AS vegplotiidref,
vegplotrefecmdoc.seqnum AS seqnum,
CODELABEL (ecmdoctype) AS ecmdoctype,
vegplotrefecmdoc.ecmdocname AS ecmdocname,
vegplotrefecmdoc.ecmdockeyurl AS ecmdockeyurl,
vegplotrefecmdoc.recwlupdated AS recwlupdated,
vegplotrefecmdoc.recuseriidref/1 AS recuseriidref,
vegplotrefecmdoc.vegplotrefecmdociid/1 AS vegplotrefecmdociid

FROM pedon
INNER JOIN siteobs ON siteobs.siteiidref=site.siteiid
INNER JOIN pedon ON pedon.siteobsiidref=siteobs.siteobsiid AND peiid IN ($pedonid_list)
INNER JOIN vegplotrefecmdoc ON vegplotrefecmdoc.vegplotiidref=vegplot.vegplotiid;.

TEMPLATE vegplotrefecmdoc WIDTH UNLIMITED SEPARATOR"|"
AT LEFT FIELD SEPARATOR  "",
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD,
FIELD.

SECTION WHEN AT START
HEADING
AT LEFT "@begin vegplotrefecmdoc".
END SECTION.

SECTION HEADING
USING vegplotrefecmdoc
'vegplotiidref',
'seqnum',
'ecmdoctype',
'ecmdocname',
'ecmdockeyurl',
'recwlupdated',
'recuseriidref',
'vegplotrefecmdociid'.

DATA
USING vegplotrefecmdoc
vegplotiidref,
seqnum,
ecmdoctype,
ecmdocname,
ecmdockeyurl,
recwlupdated,
recuseriidref,
vegplotrefecmdociid.
END SECTION.

SECTION WHEN NO DATA
DATA
AT LEFT "@begin vegplotrefecmdoc".
USING vegplotrefecmdoc
'vegplotiidref',
'seqnum',
'ecmdoctype',
'ecmdocname',
'ecmdockeyurl',
'recwlupdated',
'recuseriidref',
'vegplotrefecmdociid'.
AT LEFT "@end".
END SECTION.

SECTION WHEN AT END DATA
AT LEFT "@end".
END SECTION.

ACCEPT pedonid_list.

vegplottext.recwlupdated AS recwlupdated,

vegplottext.vegplottextiid/1 AS vegplottextiid

FROM pedon
INNER JOIN siteobs ON siteobs.siteiidref=site.siteiid
INNER JOIN pedon ON pedon.siteobsiidref=siteobs.siteobsiid AND peiid IN ($pedonid_list)
INNER JOIN vegplottext ON vegplottext.vegplotiidref=vegplot.vegplotiid;.

NASIS Pedon Report for: vegtransecttext ---- Vegetation Transect Text

ACCEPT pedonid_list.
EXEC SQL SELECT

vegtransecttext.vegtransectiidref/1 AS vegtransectiidref,
vegtransecttext.seqnum AS seqnum,
vegtransecttext.recdate AS recdate,
vegtransecttext.recauthor AS recauthor,
CODELABEL (vegtransecttextkind) AS vegtransecttextkind,
vegtransecttext.textcat AS textcat,
vegtransecttext.textsubcat AS textsubcat,
vegtransecttext.textentry AS textentry,
vegtransecttext.recwlupdated AS recwlupdated,
vegtransecttext.recuseriidref/1 AS recuseriidref,
vegtransecttext.vegtranstextiid/1 AS vegtranstextiid

FROM pedon
INNER JOIN siteobs ON siteobs.siteiidref=site.siteiid
INNER JOIN pedon ON pedon.siteobsiidref=siteobs.siteobsiid AND peiid IN ($pedonid_list)
INNER JOIN vegtransect ON vegtransect.vegplotiidref=vegplot.vegplotiid
INNER JOIN vegtransecttext ON vegtransecttext.vegtransectiidref=vegtransect.vegtransectiid;.
